class \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_legend_a1cdf9df76adcfae45261690aa0ca2198_a1cdf9df76adcfae45261690aa0ca2198}{QCustom\+Plot}}
\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_legend_a8a375e31e42c68de049fcf0fd35db5b0_a8a375e31e42c68de049fcf0fd35db5b0}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}}
\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Manages a legend inside a \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot}. 

A legend is a small box somewhere in the plot which lists plottables with their name and icon.

A legend is populated with legend items by calling \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_plottable_aa64e93cb5b606d8110d2cc0a349bb30f_aa64e93cb5b606d8110d2cc0a349bb30f}{QCPAbstract\+Plottable\+::add\+To\+Legend} on the plottable, for which a legend item shall be created. In the case of the main legend (\doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a73da53368aa4c2db3d874cf0db50d140_a73da53368aa4c2db3d874cf0db50d140}{QCustom\+Plot\+::legend}), simply adding plottables to the plot while \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_ad8858410c2db47b7104040a3aa61c3fc_ad8858410c2db47b7104040a3aa61c3fc}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Auto\+Add\+Plottable\+To\+Legend} is set to true (the default) creates corresponding legend items. The legend item associated with a certain plottable can be removed with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_plottable_a3cc235007e2343a65ad4f463767e0e20_a3cc235007e2343a65ad4f463767e0e20}{QCPAbstract\+Plottable\+::remove\+From\+Legend}. However, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend}{QCPLegend} also offers an interface to add and manipulate legend items directly\+: \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_acfe9694c45104a3359d3806ed366fcf7_acfe9694c45104a3359d3806ed366fcf7}{item}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a91e790002d8bf15a20628a8e8841e397_a91e790002d8bf15a20628a8e8841e397}{item\+With\+Plottable}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88}{item\+Count}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a3ab274de52d2951faea45a6d975e6b3f_a3ab274de52d2951faea45a6d975e6b3f}{add\+Item}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ac91595c3eaa746fe6321d2eb952c63bb_ac91595c3eaa746fe6321d2eb952c63bb}{remove\+Item}, etc.

Since \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend}{QCPLegend} derives from \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid}, it can be placed in any position a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element} may be positioned. The legend items are themselves \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Elements} which are placed in the grid layout of the legend. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend}{QCPLegend} only adds an interface specialized for handling child elements of type \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}, as mentioned above. In principle, any other layout elements may also be added to a legend via the normal \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} interface. See the special page about \doxylink{}{The Layout System} for examples on how to add other elements to the legend and move it outside the axis rect.

Use the methods \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap} inherited from \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} to control in which order (column first or row first) the legend is filled up when calling \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a3ab274de52d2951faea45a6d975e6b3f_a3ab274de52d2951faea45a6d975e6b3f}{add\+Item}, and at which column or row wrapping occurs. The default fill order for legends is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353ccaa0202730954e26c474cc820164aedce3e}{fo\+Rows\+First}.

By default, every \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} has one legend (\doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a73da53368aa4c2db3d874cf0db50d140_a73da53368aa4c2db3d874cf0db50d140}{QCustom\+Plot\+::legend}) which is placed in the inset layout of the main axis rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a949f803466619924c7018df4b511ae10_a949f803466619924c7018df4b511ae10}{QCPAxis\+Rect\+::inset\+Layout}). To move the legend to another position inside the axis rect, use the methods of the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_inset}{QCPLayout\+Inset}. To move the legend outside of the axis rect, place it anywhere else with the QCPLayout/ \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element} interface.

Defines in which direction the grid is filled when using \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b}{add\+Element(\+QCPLayout\+Element\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})}. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!SizeConstraintRect@{SizeConstraintRect}}
\index{SizeConstraintRect@{SizeConstraintRect}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SizeConstraintRect}{SizeConstraintRect}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Defines to which rect of a layout element the size constraints that can be set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size} apply. The outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) includes the margins (e.\+g. in the case of a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} the axis labels), whereas the inner rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}) does not.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}

scr\+Inner\+Rect&Minimum/\+Maximum size constraints apply to inner rect. \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UpdatePhase}{UpdatePhase}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d}

Defines the phases of the update process, that happens just before a replot. At each phase, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_a48ecc9c98ea90b547c3e27a931a8f7bd_a48ecc9c98ea90b547c3e27a931a8f7bd}{update} is called with the according Update\+Phase value. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{upPreparation@{upPreparation}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!upPreparation@{upPreparation}}}\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374dad6119882eba136357c2f627992e527d3}\label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d} 
up\+Preparation&Phase used for any type of preparation that needs to be done before margin calculation and layout. \\

\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!addElement@{addElement}}
\index{addElement@{addElement}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addElement()}{addElement()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012} 
bool QCPLayout\+Grid\+::add\+Element (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{row}{, }\item[{int}]{column}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{element}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Adds the {\itshape element} to cell with {\itshape row} and {\itshape column}. If {\itshape element} is already in a layout, it is first removed from there. If {\itshape row} or {\itshape column} don\textquotesingle{}t exist yet, the layout is expanded accordingly.

Returns true if the element was added successfully, i.\+e. if the cell at {\itshape row} and {\itshape column} didn\textquotesingle{}t already have an element.

Use the overload of this method without explicit row/column index to place the element according to the configured fill order and wrapping settings.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addElement()}{addElement()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b} 
bool QCPLayout\+Grid\+::add\+Element (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{element}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Adds the {\itshape element} to the next empty cell according to the current fill order (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}) and wrapping (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap}). If {\itshape element} is already in a layout, it is first removed from there. If necessary, the layout is expanded to hold the new element.

Returns true if the element was added successfully.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_a3ab274de52d2951faea45a6d975e6b3f_a3ab274de52d2951faea45a6d975e6b3f} 
bool QCPLegend\+::add\+Item (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{item}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds {\itshape item} to the legend, if it\textquotesingle{}s not present already. The element is arranged according to the current fill order (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}) and wrapping (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap}).

Returns true on sucess, i.\+e. if the item wasn\textquotesingle{}t in the list already and has been successfuly added.

The legend takes ownership of the item.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a602b426609b4411cf6a93c3ddf3a381a_a602b426609b4411cf6a93c3ddf3a381a}

Returns the element in the cell in {\itshape row} and {\itshape column}.

Returns {\ttfamily nullptr} if either the row/column is invalid or if the cell is empty. In those cases, a q\+Debug message is printed. To check whether a cell exists and isn\textquotesingle{}t empty, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab0cf4f7edc9414a3bfaddac0f46dc0a0_ab0cf4f7edc9414a3bfaddac0f46dc0a0}{has\+Element}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d5b968b4cf57393e9e387976d91f8f7_a7d5b968b4cf57393e9e387976d91f8f7} 
QList$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$ QCPLayout\+Grid\+::elements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{recursive}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns a list of all child elements in this layout element. If {\itshape recursive} is true, all sub-\/child elements are included in the list, too.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
There may be {\ttfamily nullptr} entries in the returned list. For example, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} may have empty cells which yield {\ttfamily nullptr} at the respective index. 
\end{DoxyWarning}


Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_aca129722c019f91d3367046f80abfa77_aca129722c019f91d3367046f80abfa77}{QCPLayout}}.

\end{center}
\end{figure}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a886c0dcbabd51a45da399e044552b685_a886c0dcbabd51a45da399e044552b685}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!expandTo@{expandTo}}
\index{expandTo@{expandTo}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{expandTo()}{expandTo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a886c0dcbabd51a45da399e044552b685_a886c0dcbabd51a45da399e044552b685} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::expand\+To (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{new\+Row\+Count}{, }\item[{int}]{new\+Column\+Count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Expands the layout to have {\itshape new\+Row\+Count} rows and {\itshape new\+Column\+Count} columns. So the last valid row index will be {\itshape new\+Row\+Count-\/1}, the last valid column index will be {\itshape new\+Column\+Count-\/1}.

If the current column/row count is already larger or equal to {\itshape new\+Column\+Count/{\itshape new\+Row\+Count},} this function does nothing in that dimension.

Newly created cells are empty, new rows and columns have the stretch factor 1.

Note that upon a call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012}{add\+Element}, the layout is expanded automatically to contain the specified row and column, using this function.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a577223db920e2acb34bc1091080c76d1_a577223db920e2acb34bc1091080c76d1}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!indexToRowCol@{indexToRowCol}}
\index{indexToRowCol@{indexToRowCol}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{indexToRowCol()}{indexToRowCol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a577223db920e2acb34bc1091080c76d1_a577223db920e2acb34bc1091080c76d1} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::index\+To\+Row\+Col (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{index}{, }\item[{int \&}]{row}{, }\item[{int \&}]{column}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Converts the linear index to row and column indices and writes the result to {\itshape row} and {\itshape column}.

The way the cells are indexed depends on \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}. If it is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353ccaa0202730954e26c474cc820164aedce3e}{fo\+Rows\+First}, the indices increase left to right and then top to bottom. If it is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353ccaac4cb4b796ec4822d5894b47b51627fb3}{fo\+Columns\+First}, the indices increase top to bottom and then left to right.

If there are no cells (i.\+e. column or row count is zero), sets {\itshape row} and {\itshape column} to -\/1.

For the retrieved {\itshape row} and {\itshape column} to be valid, the passed {\itshape index} must be valid itself, i.\+e. greater or equal to zero and smaller than the current \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a9a8942aface780a02445ebcf14c48513_a9a8942aface780a02445ebcf14c48513}{element\+Count}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a682ba76f130810ffd294032a1bfbcfcb_a682ba76f130810ffd294032a1bfbcfcb}{row\+Col\+To\+Index} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::insert\+Column (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{new\+Index}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Inserts a new column with empty cells at the column index {\itshape new\+Index}. Valid values for {\itshape new\+Index} range from 0 (inserts a column at the left) to {\itshape column\+Count} (appends a column at the right).

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_acfe9694c45104a3359d3806ed366fcf7_acfe9694c45104a3359d3806ed366fcf7}

Returns the item with index {\itshape i}. If non-\/legend items were added to the legend, and the element at the specified cell index is not a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}, returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

Note that the linear index depends on the current fill order (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}).

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_legend_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!itemCount@{itemCount}}
\index{itemCount@{itemCount}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{itemCount()}{itemCount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88} 
int QCPLegend\+::item\+Count (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns the number of items currently in the legend. It is identical to the base class \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a9a8942aface780a02445ebcf14c48513_a9a8942aface780a02445ebcf14c48513}{QCPLayout\+Grid\+::element\+Count()}, and unlike the other "{}item"{} interface methods of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend}{QCPLegend}, doesn\textquotesingle{}t only address elements which can be cast to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}.

Note that if empty cells are in the legend (e.\+g. by calling methods of the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} base class which allows creating empty cells), they are included in the returned count.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!maximumOuterSizeHint@{maximumOuterSizeHint}}
\index{maximumOuterSizeHint@{maximumOuterSizeHint}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{maximumOuterSizeHint()}{maximumOuterSizeHint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599} 
QSize QCPLayout\+Grid\+::maximum\+Outer\+Size\+Hint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the suggested maximum size this layout element (the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) may be expanded to, if no manual maximum size is set.

if a maximum size (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size}) was not set manually, parent layouts use the returned size (usually indirectly through \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_add49fd6843821a6126914b837ed52e22_add49fd6843821a6126914b837ed52e22}{QCPLayout\+::get\+Final\+Maximum\+Outer\+Size}) to determine the maximum allowed size of this layout element.

A manual maximum size is considered set if it is smaller than Qt\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily QWIDGETSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX}.

The default implementation simply returns {\ttfamily QWIDGETSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX} for both width and height, implying no suggested maximum size. Reimplementations may use their detailed knowledge about the layout element\textquotesingle{}s content to provide size hints. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_ad96efb977a26e360e8a64a4c1e56456d_ad96efb977a26e360e8a64a4c1e56456d}{QCPLayout\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!minimumOuterSizeHint@{minimumOuterSizeHint}}
\index{minimumOuterSizeHint@{minimumOuterSizeHint}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{minimumOuterSizeHint()}{minimumOuterSizeHint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df} 
QSize QCPLayout\+Grid\+::minimum\+Outer\+Size\+Hint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the suggested minimum size this layout element (the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) may be compressed to, if no manual minimum size is set.

if a minimum size (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size}) was not set manually, parent layouts use the returned size (usually indirectly through \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_a864fddc84721f186663faf3683f1fa70_a864fddc84721f186663faf3683f1fa70}{QCPLayout\+::get\+Final\+Minimum\+Outer\+Size}) to determine the minimum allowed size of this layout element.

A manual minimum size is considered set if it is non-\/zero.

The default implementation simply returns the sum of the horizontal margins for the width and the sum of the vertical margins for the height. Reimplementations may use their detailed knowledge about the layout element\textquotesingle{}s content to provide size hints. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09}{QCPLayout\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!mouseDoubleClickEvent@{mouseDoubleClickEvent}}
\index{mouseDoubleClickEvent@{mouseDoubleClickEvent}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseDoubleClickEvent()}{mouseDoubleClickEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81} 
void QCPLayerable\+::mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QVariant \&}]{details}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user presses the mouse button a second time in a double-\/click, while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}{select\+Test}.

The \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event} is called instead of the second \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}. So in the case of a double-\/click, the event succession is {\itshape press\+Event -- release\+Event -- double\+Click\+Event -- release\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape details} contains layerable-\/specific details about the hit, which were generated in the previous call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}{select\+Test}. For example, One-\/dimensional plottables like \doxylink{class_q_c_p_graph}{QCPGraph} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_bars}{QCPBars} convey the clicked data point in the {\itshape details} parameter, as \doxylink{class_q_c_p_data_selection}{QCPData\+Selection} packed as QVariant. Multi-\/part objects convey the specific {\ttfamily Selectable\+Part} that was hit (e.\+g. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f}{QCPAxis\+::\+Selectable\+Part} in the case of axes).

Similarly to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, once a layerable has accepted the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, it is considered the mouse grabber and will receive all following calls to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4}{mouse\+Move\+Event} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c}{mouse\+Release\+Event} for this mouse interaction (a "{}mouse interaction"{} in this context ends with the release).

The default implementation does nothing except explicitly ignoring the event with {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_a2272ff775ab385f612e9fd39773de7c0_a2272ff775ab385f612e9fd39773de7c0}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!mouseMoveEvent@{mouseMoveEvent}}
\index{mouseMoveEvent@{mouseMoveEvent}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseMoveEvent()}{mouseMoveEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4} 
void QCPLayerable\+::mouse\+Move\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QPointF \&}]{start\+Pos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user moves the mouse while holding a mouse button, after this layerable has become the mouse grabber by accepting the preceding \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape start\+Pos} indicates the position where the initial \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event} occurred, that started the mouse interaction.

The default implementation does nothing.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_ac5a269609e6177737faabdc46434d8c7_ac5a269609e6177737faabdc46434d8c7}{QCPAxis}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{QCPAxis\+Rect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_a3b2bd79725aefaf2630fc76e90939442_a3b2bd79725aefaf2630fc76e90939442}{QCPColor\+Scale}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{QCPColor\+Scale\+Axis\+Rect\+Private}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_radial_acaaca448f4599cc4d8b4d6a35f61e1e6_acaaca448f4599cc4d8b4d6a35f61e1e6}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Radial}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!mousePressEvent@{mousePressEvent}}
\index{mousePressEvent@{mousePressEvent}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mousePressEvent()}{mousePressEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376} 
void QCPLayerable\+::mouse\+Press\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QVariant \&}]{details}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user presses a mouse button while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}{select\+Test}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape details} contains layerable-\/specific details about the hit, which were generated in the previous call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}{select\+Test}. For example, One-\/dimensional plottables like \doxylink{class_q_c_p_graph}{QCPGraph} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_bars}{QCPBars} convey the clicked data point in the {\itshape details} parameter, as \doxylink{class_q_c_p_data_selection}{QCPData\+Selection} packed as QVariant. Multi-\/part objects convey the specific {\ttfamily Selectable\+Part} that was hit (e.\+g. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f}{QCPAxis\+::\+Selectable\+Part} in the case of axes).

\doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} uses an event propagation system that works the same as Qt\textquotesingle{}s system. If your layerable doesn\textquotesingle{}t reimplement the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event} or explicitly calls {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()} in its reimplementation, the event will be propagated to the next layerable in the stacking order.

Once a layerable has accepted the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, it is considered the mouse grabber and will receive all following calls to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4}{mouse\+Move\+Event} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c}{mouse\+Release\+Event} for this mouse interaction (a "{}mouse interaction"{} in this context ends with the release).

The default implementation does nothing except explicitly ignoring the event with {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4_a9eee1ba47fd69be111059ca3881933e4}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_a61bc07cda6193a3fa6b5aa198fc4e4fa_a61bc07cda6193a3fa6b5aa198fc4e4fa}{QCPAxis}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{QCPAxis\+Rect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_a91f633b97ffcd57fdf8cd814974c20e6_a91f633b97ffcd57fdf8cd814974c20e6}{QCPColor\+Scale}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{QCPColor\+Scale\+Axis\+Rect\+Private}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_radial_a0fa3d3c617a57b4115b9bec55b739f88_a0fa3d3c617a57b4115b9bec55b739f88}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Radial}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_ad7b2c98355e3d2f912574b74fcee0574_ad7b2c98355e3d2f912574b74fcee0574}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!mouseReleaseEvent@{mouseReleaseEvent}}
\index{mouseReleaseEvent@{mouseReleaseEvent}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseReleaseEvent()}{mouseReleaseEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c_aa0d79b005686f668622bbe66ac03ba2c} 
void QCPLayerable\+::mouse\+Release\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QPointF \&}]{start\+Pos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user releases the mouse button, after this layerable has become the mouse grabber by accepting the preceding \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape start\+Pos} indicates the position where the initial \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376_af6567604818db90f4fd52822f8bc8376}{mouse\+Press\+Event} occurred, that started the mouse interaction.

The default implementation does nothing.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!outerRect@{outerRect}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{outerRect()}{outerRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c} 
QRect QCPLayout\+Element\+::outer\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the outer rect of this layout element. The outer rect is the inner rect expanded by the margins (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}). The outer rect is used (and set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) by the parent \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout}{QCPLayout} to control the size of this layout element.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!parentLayerable@{parentLayerable}}
\index{parentLayerable@{parentLayerable}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parentLayerable()}{parentLayerable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layerable}{QCPLayerable}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} QCPLayerable\+::parent\+Layerable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the parent layerable of this layerable. The parent layerable is used to provide visibility hierarchies in conjunction with the method \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}{real\+Visibility}. This way, layerables only get drawn if their parent layerables are visible, too.

Note that a parent layerable is not necessarily also the QObject parent for memory management. Further, a layerable doesn\textquotesingle{}t always have a parent layerable, so this function may return {\ttfamily nullptr}.

A parent layerable is set implicitly when placed inside layout elements and doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be set manually by the user. Here is the caller graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]
\begin{center}
\leavevmode

\end{center}
\end{figure}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!realVisibility@{realVisibility}}
\index{realVisibility@{realVisibility}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{realVisibility()}{realVisibility()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7} 
bool QCPLayerable\+::real\+Visibility (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns whether this layerable is visible, taking the visibility of the layerable parent and the visibility of this layerable\textquotesingle{}s layer into account. This is the method that is consulted to decide whether a layerable shall be drawn or not.

If this layerable has a direct layerable parent (usually set via hierarchies implemented in subclasses, like in the case of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}), this function returns true only if this layerable has its visibility set to true and the parent layerable\textquotesingle{}s \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}{real\+Visibility} returns true. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!rect@{rect}}
\index{rect@{rect}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rect()}{rect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4} 
QRect QCPLayout\+Element\+::rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the inner rect of this layout element. The inner rect is the outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) shrinked by the margins (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}).

In some cases, the area between outer and inner rect is left blank. In other cases the margin area is used to display peripheral graphics while the main content is in the inner rect. This is where automatic margin calculation becomes interesting because it allows the layout element to adapt the margins to the peripheral graphics it wants to draw. For example, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} draws the axis labels and tick labels in the margin area, thus needs to adjust the margins (if \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is enabled) according to the space required by the labels of the axes.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{center}
\end{figure}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_a6c58f537d8086f352576ab7c5b15d0bc_a6c58f537d8086f352576ab7c5b15d0bc}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!remove@{remove}}
\index{remove@{remove}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{remove()}{remove()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_a6c58f537d8086f352576ab7c5b15d0bc_a6c58f537d8086f352576ab7c5b15d0bc} 
bool QCPLayout\+::remove (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{element}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Removes and deletes the provided {\itshape element}. Returns true on success. If {\itshape element} is not in the layout, returns false.

This function internally uses \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a17dd220234d1bbf8835abcc666384d45_a17dd220234d1bbf8835abcc666384d45}{take\+At} to remove the element from the layout and then deletes the element. Note that some layouts don\textquotesingle{}t remove the respective cell right away but leave an empty cell after successful removal of the layout element. To collapse empty cells, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a38621ca7aa633b6a9a88617df7f08672_a38621ca7aa633b6a9a88617df7f08672}{simplify}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_a2403f684fee3ce47132faaeed00bb066_a2403f684fee3ce47132faaeed00bb066}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!removeAt@{removeAt}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{removeAt()}{removeAt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_a2403f684fee3ce47132faaeed00bb066_a2403f684fee3ce47132faaeed00bb066} 
bool QCPLayout\+::remove\+At (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{index}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Removes and deletes the element at the provided {\itshape index}. Returns true on success. If {\itshape index} is invalid or points to an empty cell, returns false.

This function internally uses \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a17dd220234d1bbf8835abcc666384d45_a17dd220234d1bbf8835abcc666384d45}{take\+At} to remove the element from the layout and then deletes the returned element. Note that some layouts don\textquotesingle{}t remove the respective cell right away but leave an empty cell after successful removal of the layout element. To collapse empty cells, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a38621ca7aa633b6a9a88617df7f08672_a38621ca7aa633b6a9a88617df7f08672}{simplify}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_legend_ac91595c3eaa746fe6321d2eb952c63bb_ac91595c3eaa746fe6321d2eb952c63bb}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!removeItem@{removeItem}}
\index{removeItem@{removeItem}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{removeItem()}{removeItem()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_ac91595c3eaa746fe6321d2eb952c63bb_ac91595c3eaa746fe6321d2eb952c63bb} 
bool QCPLegend\+::remove\+Item (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{index}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Removes the item with the specified {\itshape index} from the legend and deletes it.

After successful removal, the legend is reordered according to the current fill order (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}) and wrapping (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap}), so no empty cell remains where the removed {\itshape item} was. If you don\textquotesingle{}t want this, rather use the raw element interface of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid}.

Returns true, if successful. Unlike \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_a2403f684fee3ce47132faaeed00bb066_a2403f684fee3ce47132faaeed00bb066}{QCPLayout\+Grid\+::remove\+At}, this method only removes elements derived from \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88_a57ab86ab8b2a3762d4c1455eb5452c88}{item\+Count}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a24795c7250eb5214fcea16b7217b4dfb_a24795c7250eb5214fcea16b7217b4dfb}{clear\+Items} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_legend_a2aea4ec6da2d454dd0b241a254d65082_a2aea4ec6da2d454dd0b241a254d65082}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!removeItem@{removeItem}}
\index{removeItem@{removeItem}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{removeItem()}{removeItem()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_a2aea4ec6da2d454dd0b241a254d65082_a2aea4ec6da2d454dd0b241a254d65082} 
bool QCPLegend\+::remove\+Item (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{item}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Removes {\itshape item} from the legend and deletes it.

After successful removal, the legend is reordered according to the current fill order (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}) and wrapping (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap}), so no empty cell remains where the removed {\itshape item} was. If you don\textquotesingle{}t want this, rather use the raw element interface of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid}.

Returns true, if successful.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a682ba76f130810ffd294032a1bfbcfcb_a682ba76f130810ffd294032a1bfbcfcb}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!rowColToIndex@{rowColToIndex}}
\index{rowColToIndex@{rowColToIndex}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rowColToIndex()}{rowColToIndex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a682ba76f130810ffd294032a1bfbcfcb_a682ba76f130810ffd294032a1bfbcfcb} 
int QCPLayout\+Grid\+::row\+Col\+To\+Index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{row}{, }\item[{int}]{column}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Converts the given {\itshape row} and {\itshape column} to the linear index used by some methods of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout}{QCPLayout}.

The way the cells are indexed depends on \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}. If it is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353ccaa0202730954e26c474cc820164aedce3e}{fo\+Rows\+First}, the indices increase left to right and then top to bottom. If it is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353ccaac4cb4b796ec4822d5894b47b51627fb3}{fo\+Columns\+First}, the indices increase top to bottom and then left to right.

For the returned index to be valid, {\itshape row} and {\itshape column} must be valid indices themselves, i.\+e. greater or equal to zero and smaller than the current row\+Count/ column\+Count.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!selectTest@{selectTest}}
\index{selectTest@{selectTest}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{selectTest()}{selectTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84} 
double QCPLegend\+::select\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPointF \&}]{pos}{, }\item[{bool}]{only\+Selectable}{, }\item[{QVariant \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{details}{ = {\ttfamily nullptr}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Layout elements are sensitive to events inside their outer rect. If {\itshape pos} is within the outer rect, this method returns a value corresponding to 0.\+99 times the parent plot\textquotesingle{}s selection tolerance. However, layout elements are not selectable by default. So if {\itshape only\+Selectable} is true, -\/1.\+0 is returned.

See \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336}{QCPLayerable\+::select\+Test} for a general explanation of this virtual method.

\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element} subclasses may reimplement this method to provide more specific selection test behaviour. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{QCPLayout\+Element}}.

Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]
\begin{center}
\leavevmode
\includegraphics[width=350pt]{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_cgraph}
\end{center}
\end{figure}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setAntialiased@{setAntialiased}}
\index{setAntialiased@{setAntialiased}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAntialiased()}{setAntialiased()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581_a4fd43e89be4a553ead41652565ff0581} 
void QCPLayerable\+::set\+Antialiased (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets whether this object will be drawn antialiased or not.

Note that antialiasing settings may be overridden by \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8_af6f91e5eab1be85f67c556e98c3745e8}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Antialiased\+Elements} and \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24_ae10d685b5eabea2999fb8775ca173c24}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Not\+Antialiased\+Elements}. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setAutoMargins@{setAutoMargins}}
\index{setAutoMargins@{setAutoMargins}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAutoMargins()}{setAutoMargins()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Auto\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Sides}]{sides}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets on which sides the margin shall be calculated automatically. If a side is calculated automatically, a minimum margin value may be provided with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673}{set\+Minimum\+Margins}. If a side is set to be controlled manually, the value may be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}.

Margin sides that are under automatic control may participate in a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group} (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d}{set\+Margin\+Group}), to synchronize (align) it with other layout elements in the plot.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ae38f31a71687b9d7ee3104852528fb50_ae38f31a71687b9d7ee3104852528fb50}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setColumnStretchFactor@{setColumnStretchFactor}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setColumnStretchFactor()}{setColumnStretchFactor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ae38f31a71687b9d7ee3104852528fb50_ae38f31a71687b9d7ee3104852528fb50} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::set\+Column\+Stretch\+Factor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{column}{, }\item[{double}]{factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the stretch {\itshape factor} of {\itshape column}.

Stretch factors control the relative sizes of rows and columns. Cells will not be resized beyond their minimum and maximum widths/heights, regardless of the stretch factor. (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Maximum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}.)

The default stretch factor of newly created rows/columns is 1.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a6c2591d1a7e2534ce036989543b49e57_a6c2591d1a7e2534ce036989543b49e57}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setColumnStretchFactors@{setColumnStretchFactors}}
\index{setColumnStretchFactors@{setColumnStretchFactors}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a6c2591d1a7e2534ce036989543b49e57_a6c2591d1a7e2534ce036989543b49e57} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::set\+Column\+Stretch\+Factors (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QList$<$ double $>$ \&}]{factors}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the stretch {\itshape factors} of all columns. {\itshape factors} must have the size \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a1a2962cbf45011405b64b913afa8e7a2_a1a2962cbf45011405b64b913afa8e7a2}{column\+Count}.

Stretch factors control the relative sizes of rows and columns. Cells will not be resized beyond their minimum and maximum widths/heights, regardless of the stretch factor. (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Maximum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}.)

The default stretch factor of newly created rows/columns is 1.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setFillOrder@{setFillOrder}}
\index{setFillOrder@{setFillOrder}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFillOrder()}{setFillOrder()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::set\+Fill\+Order (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca}{Fill\+Order}}}]{order}{, }\item[{bool}]{rearrange}{ = {\ttfamily true}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the filling order and wrapping behaviour that is used when adding new elements with the method \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b}{add\+Element(\+QCPLayout\+Element\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})}.

The specified {\itshape order} defines whether rows or columns are filled first. Using \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap}, you can control at which row/column count wrapping into the next column/row will occur. If you set it to zero, no wrapping will ever occur. Changing the fill order also changes the meaning of the linear index used e.\+g. in \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a4288f174082555f6bd92021bdedb75dc_a4288f174082555f6bd92021bdedb75dc}{element\+At} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a17dd220234d1bbf8835abcc666384d45_a17dd220234d1bbf8835abcc666384d45}{take\+At}. The default fill order for \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353cca_a7d49ee08773de6b2fd246edfed353ccaac4cb4b796ec4822d5894b47b51627fb3}{fo\+Columns\+First}.

If you want to have all current elements arranged in the new order, set {\itshape rearrange} to true. The elements will be rearranged in a way that tries to preserve their linear index. However, empty cells are skipped during build-\/up of the new cell order, which shifts the succeeding element\textquotesingle{}s index. The rearranging is performed even if the specified {\itshape order} is already the current fill order. Thus this method can be used to re-\/wrap the current elements.

If {\itshape rearrange} is false, the current element arrangement is not changed, which means the linear indexes change (because the linear index is dependent on the fill order).

Note that the method \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012}{add\+Element(int row, int column, QCPLayout\+Element \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}element)} with explicitly stated row and column is not subject to wrapping and can place elements even beyond the specified wrapping point.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}{set\+Wrap}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b}{add\+Element(\+QCPLayout\+Element\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Sets the default font of legend text. Legend items that draw text (e.\+g. the name of a graph) will use this font by default. However, a different font can be specified on a per-\/item-\/basis by accessing the specific legend item.

This function will also set {\itshape font} on all already existing legend items.

bool QCPLayerable\+::set\+Layer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layer}{QCPLayer}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{layer}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the {\itshape layer} of this layerable object. The object will be placed on top of the other objects already on {\itshape layer}.

If {\itshape layer} is 0, this layerable will not be on any layer and thus not appear in the plot (or interact/receive events).

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Margin\+Group (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Sides}]{sides}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{group}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the margin {\itshape group} of the specified margin {\itshape sides}.

Margin groups allow synchronizing specified margins across layout elements, see the documentation of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group}.

To unset the margin group of {\itshape sides}, set {\itshape group} to {\ttfamily nullptr}.

Note that margin groups only work for margin sides that are set to automatic (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMargins()}{setMargins()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QMargins \&}]{margins}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the margins of this layout element. If \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is disabled for some or all sides, this function is used to manually set the margin on those sides. Sides that are still set to be handled automatically are ignored and may have any value in {\itshape margins}.

The margin is the distance between the outer rect (controlled by the parent layout via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) and the inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} (which usually contains the main content of this layout element).

void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QMargins \&}]{margins}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

The minimum values are not enforced on margin sides that were set to be under manual control via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setMinimumSize@{setMinimumSize}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMinimumSize()}{setMinimumSize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QSize \&}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the minimum size of this layout element. A parent layout tries to respect the {\itshape size} here by changing row/column sizes in the layout accordingly.

If the parent layout size is not sufficient to satisfy all minimum size constraints of its child layout elements, the layout may set a size that is actually smaller than {\itshape size}. \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} propagates the layout\textquotesingle{}s size constraints to the outside by setting its own minimum QWidget size accordingly, so violations of {\itshape size} should be exceptions.

Whether this constraint applies to the inner or the outer rect can be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect} (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}). \doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setOuterRect()}{setOuterRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Outer\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QRect \&}]{rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the outer rect of this layout element. If the layout element is inside a layout, the layout sets the position and size of this layout element using this function.

Calling this function externally has no effect, since the layout will overwrite any changes to the outer rect upon the next replot.

The layout element will adapt its inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} by applying the margins inward to the outer rect.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7b0273de5369bd93d942edbaf5b166ec_a7b0273de5369bd93d942edbaf5b166ec}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setRowStretchFactor@{setRowStretchFactor}}
\index{setRowStretchFactor@{setRowStretchFactor}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRowStretchFactor()}{setRowStretchFactor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7b0273de5369bd93d942edbaf5b166ec_a7b0273de5369bd93d942edbaf5b166ec} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::set\+Row\+Stretch\+Factor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{row}{, }\item[{double}]{factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the stretch {\itshape factor} of {\itshape row}.

Stretch factors control the relative sizes of rows and columns. Cells will not be resized beyond their minimum and maximum widths/heights, regardless of the stretch factor. (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Maximum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}.)

The default stretch factor of newly created rows/columns is 1.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a6c2591d1a7e2534ce036989543b49e57_a6c2591d1a7e2534ce036989543b49e57}{set\+Column\+Stretch\+Factors}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a7b0273de5369bd93d942edbaf5b166ec_a7b0273de5369bd93d942edbaf5b166ec}{set\+Row\+Stretch\+Factor}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a200b45f9c908f96ebadaa3c8d87a2782_a200b45f9c908f96ebadaa3c8d87a2782} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::set\+Row\+Stretch\+Factors (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QList$<$ double $>$ \&}]{factors}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the stretch {\itshape factors} of all rows. {\itshape factors} must have the size \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a19c66fd76cbce58a8e94f33797e0c0aa_a19c66fd76cbce58a8e94f33797e0c0aa}{row\+Count}.

Stretch factors control the relative sizes of rows and columns. Cells will not be resized beyond their minimum and maximum widths/heights, regardless of the stretch factor. (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Maximum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}.)

The default stretch factor of newly created rows/columns is 1.

void QCPLegend\+::set\+Selectable\+Parts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Selectable\+Parts \&}]{selectable}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether the user can (de-\/)select the parts in {\itshape selectable} by clicking on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} surface. (When \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} contains \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037a269c9af298e257d1108edec0432b5513}{QCP\+::i\+Select\+Legend}.)

However, even when {\itshape selectable} is set to a value not allowing the selection of a specific part, it is still possible to set the selection of this part manually, by calling \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a2aee309bb5c2a794b1987f3fc97f8ad8_a2aee309bb5c2a794b1987f3fc97f8ad8}{set\+Selected\+Parts} directly.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_legend_a2aee309bb5c2a794b1987f3fc97f8ad8_a2aee309bb5c2a794b1987f3fc97f8ad8}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setSelectedParts@{setSelectedParts}}
\index{setSelectedParts@{setSelectedParts}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSelectedParts()}{setSelectedParts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_a2aee309bb5c2a794b1987f3fc97f8ad8_a2aee309bb5c2a794b1987f3fc97f8ad8} 
void QCPLegend\+::set\+Selected\+Parts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Selectable\+Parts \&}]{selected}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the selected state of the respective legend parts described by \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1}{Selectable\+Part}. When a part is selected, it uses a different pen/font and brush. If some legend items are selected and {\itshape selected} doesn\textquotesingle{}t contain \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1a768bfb95f323db4c66473375032c0af7}{sp\+Items}, those items become deselected.

The entire selection mechanism is handled automatically when \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} contains i\+Select\+Legend. You only need to call this function when you wish to change the selection state manually.

This function can change the selection state of a part even when \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a9ce60aa8bbd89f62ae4fa83ac6c60110_a9ce60aa8bbd89f62ae4fa83ac6c60110}{set\+Selectable\+Parts} was set to a value that actually excludes the part.

emits the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a82c88464edac07a9eefaf3906268df3b_a82c88464edac07a9eefaf3906268df3b}{selection\+Changed} signal when {\itshape selected} is different from the previous selection state.

Note that it doesn\textquotesingle{}t make sense to set the selected state \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1a768bfb95f323db4c66473375032c0af7}{sp\+Items} here when it wasn\textquotesingle{}t set before, because there\textquotesingle{}s no way to specify which exact items to newly select. Do this by calling \doxylink{class_q_c_p_abstract_legend_item_a6eed93b0ab99cb3eabb043fb08179c2b_a6eed93b0ab99cb3eabb043fb08179c2b}{QCPAbstract\+Legend\+Item\+::set\+Selected} directly on the legend item you wish to select.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1_a5404de8bc1e4a994ca4ae69e2c7072f1}{Selectable\+Part}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a9ce60aa8bbd89f62ae4fa83ac6c60110_a9ce60aa8bbd89f62ae4fa83ac6c60110}{set\+Selectable\+Parts}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}{select\+Test}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a2c35d262953a25d96b6112653fbefc88_a2c35d262953a25d96b6112653fbefc88}{set\+Selected\+Border\+Pen}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ade93aabe9bcccaf9cf46cec22c658027_ade93aabe9bcccaf9cf46cec22c658027}{set\+Selected\+Icon\+Border\+Pen}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_a875227f3219c9799464631dec5e8f1bd_a875227f3219c9799464631dec5e8f1bd}{set\+Selected\+Brush}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ab580a01c3c0a239374ed66c29edf5ad2_ab580a01c3c0a239374ed66c29edf5ad2}{set\+Selected\+Font} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setSizeConstraintRect@{setSizeConstraintRect}}
\index{setSizeConstraintRect@{setSizeConstraintRect}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSizeConstraintRect()}{setSizeConstraintRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}{Size\+Constraint\+Rect}}}]{constraint\+Rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets to which rect of a layout element the size constraints apply. Size constraints can be set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size}.

The outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) includes the margins (e.\+g. in the case of a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} the axis labels), whereas the inner rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}) does not.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_legend_ae1eb239ff4a4632fe1b6c3e668d845c6_ae1eb239ff4a4632fe1b6c3e668d845c6} 
void QCPLegend\+::set\+Text\+Color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QColor \&}]{color}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the default color of legend text. Legend items that draw text (e.\+g. the name of a graph) will use this color by default. However, a different colors can be specified on a per-\/item-\/basis by accessing the specific legend item.

This function will also set {\itshape color} on all already existing legend items.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!setWrap@{setWrap}}
\index{setWrap@{setWrap}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setWrap()}{setWrap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598_ab36af18d77e4428386d02970382ee598} 
void QCPLayout\+Grid\+::set\+Wrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the maximum number of columns or rows that are used, before new elements added with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b_a4c44025dd25acd27e053cadfd448ad7b}{add\+Element(\+QCPLayout\+Element\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})} will start to fill the next row or column, respectively. It depends on \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order}, whether rows or columns are wrapped.

If {\itshape count} is set to zero, no wrapping will ever occur.

If you wish to re-\/wrap the elements currently in the layout, call \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391_affc2f3cfd22f28698c5b29b960d2a391}{set\+Fill\+Order} with {\itshape rearrange} set to true (the actual fill order doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be changed for the rearranging to be done).

Note that the method \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012_adff1a2ca691ed83d2d24a4cd1fe17012}{add\+Element(int row, int column, QCPLayout\+Element \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}element)} with explicitly stated row and column is not subject to wrapping and can place elements even beyond the specified wrapping point.

Subclasses call this method to report changed (minimum/maximum) size constraints.

If the parent of this layout is again a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout}{QCPLayout}, forwards the call to the parent\textquotesingle{}s \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_aeac66a292f65cf7f8adf94eb92345b3e_aeac66a292f65cf7f8adf94eb92345b3e}{size\+Constraints\+Changed}. If the parent is a QWidget (i.\+e. is the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_af1a1f1f571237deb7c2bd34a5e9f018f_af1a1f1f571237deb7c2bd34a5e9f018f}{QCustom\+Plot\+::plot\+Layout} of \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot}), calls QWidget\+::update\+Geometry, so if the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is inside a Qt QLayout, it may update itself and resize cells accordingly. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_aee961c2eb6cf8a85dcbc5a7d7b6c1a00_aee961c2eb6cf8a85dcbc5a7d7b6c1a00}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!take@{take}}
\index{take@{take}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{take()}{take()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_aee961c2eb6cf8a85dcbc5a7d7b6c1a00_aee961c2eb6cf8a85dcbc5a7d7b6c1a00} 
bool QCPLayout\+Grid\+::take (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{element}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Removes the specified {\itshape element} from the layout and returns true on success.

If the {\itshape element} isn\textquotesingle{}t in this layout, returns false.

Note that some layouts don\textquotesingle{}t remove the respective cell right away but leave an empty cell after successful removal of the layout element. To collapse empty cells, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a38621ca7aa633b6a9a88617df7f08672_a38621ca7aa633b6a9a88617df7f08672}{simplify}.

If {\itshape phase} is \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374da5d1ccf5d79967c232c3c511796860045}{up\+Layout}, calls \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a6cf43f14d3fa335fd8758561ccf1f78c_a6cf43f14d3fa335fd8758561ccf1f78c}{update\+Layout}, which subclasses may reimplement to reposition and resize their cells.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022}\index{QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}!wheelEvent@{wheelEvent}}
\index{wheelEvent@{wheelEvent}!QCPLegend@{QCPLegend}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wheelEvent()}{wheelEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022_a47dfd7b8fd99c08ca54e09c362b6f022} 
void QCPLayerable\+::wheel\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QWheel\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user turns the mouse scroll wheel while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_legend_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84_ae11e1229abeec1abdbd22a57f2b26a84}{select\+Test}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}.

The {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}angle\+Delta()} indicates how far the mouse wheel was turned, which is usually +/-\/ 120 for single rotation steps. However, if the mouse wheel is turned rapidly, multiple steps may accumulate to one event, making the delta larger. On the other hand, if the wheel has very smooth steps or none at all, the delta may be smaller.

The default implementation does nothing.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
